beginSubroutine: s32'WFree_KobetsuFunc'
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(2)
    isObjectActive: (STACK1)
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      sendSignal: (STACK1), (SIGNAL1)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'Damage_SetDispMesh_Check'
  returnValue: 0, 0
  checkLastAttackHitStateName: 3, s32'ZanseiRouga'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    returnValue: 0, 1
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'Damage_SetDispMesh'
